Arrival Information
Subjective
Patient is a 33 year old female that presents status post L distal radius fracture (ORIF). Although she is right handed, she notes that
she is has difficulty with gripping, fifting, wrist ROM, and global use of herLUE. She notes that on 12/5 she was working at Sonic
when she misstopped and had a FOOSH injury. She had surgery on 12/7 and will follow upon 1/30. She notes that she is unable to
move her fingers well secondary to swelling and N/T into 3-4 finger going up into the outside of herelbow. She is now sleeping in
her bed but has been sleeping onthe couch due to discomfort.

Assessment
Assessment
The pleasant 33 y/o femate patient appears before physical therapy this date with reports of L wrist stiffness, loss of ROM,
decreased use for ADL's and IADL's secondary to decreased dexterity and strength, as well as N/T in ulnar aspect distribution.
Upon assessment, the patient's s/s are consistent with status past L ORIF of radius. Patient presents with moderate swelling and
severe limitations in ROM, mobility, and decreased arthrokinematics of elbow and wrist five weeks post op. Concerns regarding
end ranges of elbow flexion, supination, as well as global mobility of MCP’s +wrist. The patient is appropriate for and would
benefit from skilled physical therapy to address deficits listed above. The patient was educated onand is in agreement with the
goals established and the physical therapy plan of care to ensue. The patient consents to physical therapy treatment. There are
nocontraindications to beginning physical therapy atthis time.
is
Good potential to reach and maintain prior level of function

Clinician Established Goals
Long Term Goals
1.Patient will have improved QuickDash score ofat least 10%.
2.Patient will demonstrate L wrist MMT globally to >5-/5 to ensure stabilization and strength
required for lifting, pushing/pulling, as well as picking up items in LUE forwork duties..
3. Patient will demonstrate L supination to70* to increase wrist ROM and mobility fordexterity
required for clasping bra or putting uphair..
4. Patient will demonstrate L wrist flexion and extension to 75* ta increase ROM required for
picking upitems overhead and above waist height without instability in wrist..
Short Term Goals
1. Patient will report reduced pain by atleast 50% with frequency ar intensity of symptoms. by
2/10/2023.
2. Patient will demonstrate independence with an advanced home exercise program to help
achieve gaals below. by 2/10/2023.
3. Patient will demonstrate L elbow flexion to 130* in pain free ranges to ensure increased
mobility forproximat joint mobility during ADL's. by 2/10/2023.
4, Patient will demonstrate the ability to sleep through the night without being awoken by pain/
discomfort. by 2/10/2023.
